There is also a capsule coffee machine and free coffee capsules in the room. There are rich varieties of welcome fruits. After checking in, the waiter also brought two cups of freshly brewed green tea, which is very heartwarming.

The hotel service attitude is also very good. When checking in, the waiter immediately brought red date tea and hot towels, asked us if we drove here, and gave us parking tickets. After checking in, a waiter helped us deliver the box to the room and taught us how to turn off the Bluetooth music in the room. The waiter in the restaurant was also smiling during dinner.

The hotel's breakfast is also very rich and tastes very good. The wonton skin is thin and the filling is large, and there are many ingredients in the soup. The sunny-side-up egg is also fried just right. It was the first time that I ate oysters in the hotel breakfast, which was very fresh and tender. In addition, there are black pepper beef ribs, mixed money tripe, fried noodles, rice noodles, egg tarts, fresh juice, etc. I can't eat it all. The hotel breakfast room is not big, so when the hotel is full and breakfast is at its peak, you will need to share tables, but the waiters are very polite and actively arrange for the guests. The experience is very good.
